-   [<span data-ttu-id="cde97-817">屬性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cde97-817">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2003-r2-attributes)



| <span data-ttu-id="cde97-818">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cde97-818">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="cde97-819">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cde97-819">Value</span></span> |
